        /// <summary>
        /// Given the name of a file, return its message digest as a 32 character
        /// string of hexadecimal digits.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="pstrFileName">
        /// String containing the message to be digested. See Remarks for
        /// important information about the internal implementation.
        /// </param>
        /// <returns>
        /// The message digest, consisting of a string of 32 hexadecimal
        /// characters. This string is identical with the strings returned by
        /// the reference implementation, published by Dr. Ronald Rivest, who is
        /// credited with inventing the SHA256 digest algrorithm.
        /// </returns>
        ///<remarks>
        /// Since the internal hashing implementations expect byte arrays, the
        /// input string must be converted. The Encoding.Default.GetBytes method
        /// is called upon to convert the string into a byte array.
        /// 
        /// A slightly modified version of the Rivest code, written in ANSI C,
        /// is the engine in my SHA256WIN stand-alone program and my SHA256Digest
        /// Windows Dynamic Link Library.
        /// 
        /// However, this function uses a SHA256CryptoServiceProvider object, which
        /// provides a managed interface to the Cryptographic Service Provider
        /// in the host's installation of Microsoft Windows. I chose this over
        /// the 100% managed implementation for two reasons.
        /// 
        /// 1) The CSP implementation uses native machine code for the
        /// computation, and should outperform managed code on large plaintexts.
        /// 
        /// 2) By using the native implementation, the CLR is eliminated as a
        /// potential point of failure due to a weakness in the implementation
        /// of the algorithm.
        ///</remarks>
        public static string SHA256Hash ( string pstrFileName )
        {
            //	Create a new instance of the SHA256CryptoServiceProvider object.

            SHA256 SHA256Hasher = new SHA256CryptoServiceProvider ( );

            //	Convert the pstrInput string to a byte array and compute the hash.

            using ( SHA256Hasher )
            {
                byte [ ] bytInputData = ProcessFile (
                    pstrFileName ,
                    SHA256Hasher );
                return DigestToHexDigits ( bytInputData );
            }	// using ( SHA256Hasher )
        }   // public static string SHA256Hash

06/28/2014 13:48:17

        /// <summary>
        /// Given the name of a file, return its SHA-1 message digest as a 32 
        /// character string of hexadecimal digits.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="pstrFileName">
        /// String containing the message to be digested.
        /// </param>
        /// <returns>
        /// The message digest, consisting of a string of 40 hexadecimal
        /// characters.
        /// </returns>
        public static string SHA256Hash ( string pstrFileName )
        {
            //	Create a new instance of the SHA256CryptoServiceProvider object.

            SHA256 SHA256Hasher = new SHA256CryptoServiceProvider ( );

            //	Convert the pstrInput string to a byte array and compute the hash.

            using ( SHA256Hasher )
            {
                byte [ ] bytInputData = SHA256Hasher.ComputeHash (
                    new FileStream (
                        pstrFileName ,
                        FileMode.Open ,
                        FileAccess.Read ,
                        FileShare.Read ,
                        BUFSIZE ,
                        FileOptions.SequentialScan 
                        | FileOptions.Asynchronous ) );
                return DigestToHexDigits ( bytInputData );
            }	// using ( SHA256Hasher )
        }   // public static string SHA256Hash


================================================================================
06/28/2014 13:57:55
================================================================================

        /// <summary>
        /// Given the name of a file, return its SHA-1 message digest as a 64 
        /// character string of hexadecimal digits.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="pstrFileName">
        /// String containing the message to be digested.
        /// </param>
        /// <returns>
        /// The message digest, consisting of a string of 64 hexadecimal
        /// characters.
        /// </returns>
        public static string SHA512Hash ( string pstrFileName )
        {
            SHA512 SHA512Hasher = new SHA512Managed ( );

            using ( SHA512Hasher )
            {
                byte [ ] bytInputData = SHA512Hasher.ComputeHash (
                    new FileStream (
                        pstrFileName ,
                        FileMode.Open ,
                        FileAccess.Read ,
                        FileShare.Read ,
                        BUFSIZE ,
                        FileOptions.SequentialScan
                        | FileOptions.Asynchronous ) );
                return DigestToHexDigits ( bytInputData );
            }	// using ( SHA512Hasher )
        }   // public static string SHA512Hash

        /// <summary>
        /// Compute the width, in characters, of the widest value in the
        /// collection.
        /// </summary>
        /// <returns>
        /// The return value is the width, in characters, of the widest value.
        /// If the class is empty, this is zero.
        /// </returns>
        public int ComputeWidthOfWidestValue ( )
        {
            int rintLongest = StandardConstants.ZERO;

            lock ( this.SyncRoot )
            {   // Create a synchronized copy, and put a padlock on it.
                foreach ( ReportDetail rd in this )
                {   // Run through the collection.
                    lock ( rd )
                    {   // Lock each member while we look at it.
                        if ( rd.Label.Length > rintLongest )
                        {   // This label is longer than any seen so far.
                            rintLongest = rd.Label.Length;
                        }   // if ( rd.Label.Length > rintLongest )
                    }   // lock ( rd )
                }   // foreach ( ReportDetail rd in this )
            }   // lock ( this.SyncRoot )

            return rintLongest;
        }   // public int ComputeWidthOfWidestValue
